Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

Page 390 

016465,000035:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016466,000036:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016467,000037:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016468,000038:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016469,000039: 
016470,000040:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016471,000041: 
016472,000042:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016473,000043:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016474,000044:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016475,000045:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016476,000046: 
016477,000047:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016478,000048:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016479,000049:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016480,000050:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016481,000051:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016482,000052: 
016483,000053:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016484,000054:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016485,000055:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016486,000056:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016487,000057: 
016488,000058:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016489,000059:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016490,000060:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016525,000095: 
016526,000096:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016527,000097: 
016528,000098:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016529,000099:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016530,000100:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016531,000101:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016532,000102:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016533,000103: 
016534,000104:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016535,000105:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016536,000106:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016537,000107:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016538,000108: 
016539,000109:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016540,000110:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016541,000111:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016542,000112:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016543,000113:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016544,000114: 
016545,000115:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016546,000116: 
016547,000117:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016548,000118:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016549,000119:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 391 

016551,000121:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016552,000122:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016553,000123:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016554,000124:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016555,000125:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016556,000126:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016557,000127:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016558,000128:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016559,000129:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016560,000130:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016561,000131: 
016562,000132:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016563,000133:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016564,000134:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016565,000135: 
016566,000136:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016567,000137: 
016568,000138:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016569,000139:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016570,000140:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016571,000141: 
016572,000142:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016573,000143:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016574,000144:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016575,000145:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016576,000146:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016577,000147:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016578,000148:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016579,000149: 
016580,000150:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016581,000151:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016582,000152: 
016583,000153:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016584,000154: 
016585,000155:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016586,000156:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016587,000157:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016588,000158:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016589,000159: 
016590,000160:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016591,000161: 
016592,000162:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016593,000163:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016594,000164:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016595,000165:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016596,000166: 
016597,000167:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 392 

016599,000169:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016600,000170: 
016601,000171:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016602,000172: 
016603,000173:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016604,000174:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
016605,000175: 
016606,000176:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016607,000177:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016608,000178:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016609,000179:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016610,000180: 
016611,000181:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016612,000182:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016613,000183: 
016614,000184:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016615,000185:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016616,000186:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016617,000187:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016618,000188: 
016619,000189:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016620,000190:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016621,000191: 
016622,000192:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016623,000193:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016624,000194: 
016625,000195:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016626,000196: 
016627,000197:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016628,000198:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016629,000199:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016630,000200:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016631,000201: 
016632,000202:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016633,000203:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016634,000204: 
016635,000205:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016636,000206:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016637,000207: 
016638,000208:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016639,000209:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016640,000210:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016641,000211:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016659,000229:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016660,000230: 
016661,000231:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016662,000232: 
016663,000233:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016664,000234:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016665,000235:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
016666,000236:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016667,000237:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016668,000238:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016669,000239:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016670,000240:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016671,000241:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016672,000242:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016673,000243:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016674,000244:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016675,000245:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016676,000246:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016677,000247:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
016678,000248:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016679,000249:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016680,000250:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016681,000251:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016682,000252:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016683,000253:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016684,000254:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016685,000255:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016686,000256:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016687,000257:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER, 11-13, C RELAYS
016688,000258:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016689,000259:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016690,000260:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016691,000261:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016692,000262:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016693,000263:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016694,000264:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016695,000265:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016696,000266:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016697,000267:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016698,000268:

016723,000293: 
016724,000294:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
016725,000295:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
016726,000296:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016727,000297:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016728,000298:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016729,000299:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
016730,000300:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016731,000301:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016732,000302:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMIN+1.
016733,000303:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016734,000304:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
016735,000305:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
016736,000306: 
016737,000307:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET        =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
016738,000308: 
016739,000309:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT         =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
016740,000310:                                                                                                  #  INREL         =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X, Y, Z, REG)
016741,000311: 
016742,000312:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM      =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

016819,000389: 
016820,000390:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016821,000391:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016822,000392:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016823,000393:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016824,000394:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016825,000395:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016826,000396: 
016827,000397:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016828,000398:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016829,000399:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016830,000400:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016831,000401:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016832,000402:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016833,000403: 
016834,000404:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016835,000405: 
016836,000406:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016837,000407:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016838,000408:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016839,000409:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016840,000410:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016841,000411:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016842,000412:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016843,000413:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016844,000414:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016845,000415:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016846,000416:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016847,000417: 
016848,000418:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016849,000419: 
016850,000420:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB                RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016851,000421:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016852,000422:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016853,000423:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016854,000424:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016855,000425:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 397 

016857,000427:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016858,000428:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016859,000429:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016860,000430:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016861,000431:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016862,000432:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016863,000433:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016864,000434:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
016865,000435: 
016866,000436:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016867,000437: 
016868,000438:                                                                                                  #  BLANK 00000
016869,000439:                                                                                                  #  0     10101
016870,000440:                                                                                                  #  1     00011
016871,000441:                                                                                                  #  2     11001
016872,000442:                                                                                                  #  3     11011
016873,000443:                                                                                                  #  4     01111
016874,000444:                                                                                                  #  5     11110
016875,000445:                                                                                                  #  6     11100
016876,000446:                                                                                                  #  7     10011
016877,000447:                                                                                                  #  8     11101
016878,000448:                                                                                                  #  9     11111
016879,000449: 
016880,000450:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016881,000451: 
016882,000452:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016883,000453:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016884,000454:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

Page 413 

017577,001147:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017578,001148: 
017579,001149:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017580,001150:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017581,001151:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017582,001152:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017583,001153:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017584,001154: 
017585,001155:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017586,001156:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017587,001157: 
017588,001158:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017589,001159: 
017590,001160:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017591,001161:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017592,001162:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017593,001163: 
017594,001164:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017595,001165:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017596,001166:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017597,001167:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017598,001168:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017599,001169:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017600,001170: 
017601,001171:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017602,001172:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017603,001173:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017604,001174:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017605,001175:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017606,001176: 
017607,001177:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017608,001178:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017609,001179: 
017610,001180:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017611,001181: 
017612,001182:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017613,001183:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017614,001184:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017615,001185:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017616,001186:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017617,001187: 
017618,001188:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017619,001189:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017620,001190:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017621,001191: 
017622,001192:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017623,001193:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017624,001194: 
017625,001195:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017626,001196:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017627,001197:

Page 414 

017629,001199:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017630,001200: 
017631,001201: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
017632,001202: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
017633,001203: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
017634,001204: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
017635,001205: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2                         
017636,001206: 41,2360           44753        DSPAB              CS       ONE

018146,001716:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

018740,002310:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018741,002311:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018742,002312:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018743,002313:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018744,002314:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018745,002315: 
018746,002316:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018747,002317:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018748,002318:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018749,002319:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018750,002320:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018751,002321:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018752,002322:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018753,002323: 
018754,002324:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018755,002325:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018756,002326:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018757,002327: 
018758,002328:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018759,002329:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018760,002330: 
018761,002331:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018762,002332:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018763,002333: 
018764,002334:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018890,002460:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018891,002461:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018892,002462:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018893,002463:                                                                                                  #  
018894,002464:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018895,002465: 
018896,002466:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018897,002467:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018898,002468:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018899,002469: 
018900,002470:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018901,002471:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018902,002472:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018903,002473: 
018904,002474: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018905,002475: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018906,002476: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018907,002477: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018908,002478: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018909,002479: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018910,002480: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWO                              
018911,002481: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019328,002898: 
019329,002899:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019330,002900: 
019331,002901:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019332,002902: 
019333,002903:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019334,002904:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019335,002905:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019336,002906:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019337,002907: 
019338,002908:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019339,002909:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019340,002910:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019341,002911: 
019342,002912:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019343,002913:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019344,002914:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019345,002915:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019346,002916:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019347,002917:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019348,002918:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019349,002919:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019350,002920:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019351,002921:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019352,002922:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019353,002923: 
019354,002924: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019355,002925: 40,3462           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019356,002926: 40,3463           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019357,002927: 40,3464           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019358,002928: 40,3465           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019359,002929: 40,3466           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019360,002930: 40,3467           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019361,002931: 40,3470           03477                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019362,002932: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019363,002933: 40,3472           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019364,002934: 40,3473           03475                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019365,002935: 40,3474           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019366,002936: 40,3475           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019367,002937: 40,3476           21050                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019368,002938: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019369,002939: 40,3500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019370,002940: 40,3501           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019371,002941: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019372,002942: 40,3503           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019373,002943: 40,3504           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019374,002944: 
019375,002945: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019376,002946:

Page 451 

019378,002948:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019379,002949:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019380,002950:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019381,002951:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019382,002952:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019383,002953: 
019384,002954:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019385,002955:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019386,002956:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019387,002957: 
019388,002958:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019389,002959:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019390,002960: 
019391,002961:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019392,002962:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019393,002963:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019394,002964:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019395,002965:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019396,002966: 
019397,002967:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019398,002968:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019399,002969:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019400,002970:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019401,002971: 
019402,002972:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019403,002973:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019404,002974:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019405,002975:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019406,002976:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019407,002977:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019408,002978:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019409,002979: 
019410,002980:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019411,002981:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019412,002982: 
019413,002983:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019414,002984:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019415,002985: 
019416,002986:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019417,002987:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019418,002988: 
019419,002989:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019420,002990:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019421,002991:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019422,002992:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019423,002993:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019424,002994:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019425,002995:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019426,002996: 
019427,002997:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 452 

019429,002999:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019430,003000:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019431,003001:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019432,003002:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019433,003003:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019434,003004:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019435,003005:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019436,003006:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019437,003007:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019438,003008: 
019439,003009:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019440,003010:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019441,003011: 
019442,003012:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019443,003013: 
019444,003014:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

019549,003119:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019550,003120: 
019551,003121:    4204                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
019552,003122:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019553,003123:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019554,003124:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019555,003125:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019556,003126:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019557,003127:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019558,003128: 
019559,003129:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019560,003130:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019561,003131:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019562,003132:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019563,003133:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019564,003134: 
019565,003135:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019566,003136:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019567,003137:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019568,003138:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019569,003139:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019570,003140:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019571,003141:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019572,003142:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019573,003143:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019574,003144:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019575,003145: 
019576,003146:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 455 

019578,003148:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019579,003149:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019580,003150:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019581,003151:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019582,003152:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019583,003153: 
019584,003154:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019585,003155:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019586,003156:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019587,003157:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019588,003158:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019589,003159:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019590,003160:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019591,003161:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019592,003162: 
019593,003163:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019594,003164: 
019595,003165:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019596,003166:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
019597,003167:    4222           00002                           TC       Q

019602,003172:    4226           00002                           TC       Q

019637,003207:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
